INC-SPECT  .Monoenergetic 60.9 - 61.9 +/- 0.1, 38.3 +/- 0.1 and   O0291  1   15 
            28.8 +/- 0.1 MeV protons, focused on the target in a  O0291  1   16 
            spot of approximately 8 mm diameter, with a walk of   O0291  1   17 
            +/- 0.4 cm. The uncertainty in number of protons      O0291  1   18 
            striking the target was +/- 1 %.                      O0291  1   19 
METHOD     (EDE) The secondary particle type was identified with  O0291  1   20 
           (TOF) A combination of delta-E versus E and flight-    O0291  1   21 
            time versus E, which permitted unambiguous            O0291  1   22 
           identification from a few MeV up to 62 MeV.            O0291  1   23 
           The low-energy cutoffs for the different particles wereO0291  1   24 
           -------------------------------------------------------O0291  1   25 
             61.5 MeV                                             O0291  1   26 
                  Protons            2.0 or 3.7 MeV               O0291  1   27

                  Helium-3                 12.4 MeV               O0291  1   30

DETECTOR   (TELES,SI,GELI) A solid state three-detector           O0291  1   45 
            telescope, with two silicon delta-E detectors and a   O0291  1   46 
            lithium-drifted germanium detector used for total     O0291  1   47 
            energy absorption. The total resolution was           O0291  1   48 
           approximately 180 keV for most of the data.            O0291  1   49 
           For the 61.5 MeV                                       O0291  1   50 
           runs the telescope was shielded by a tantalum or nickelO0291  1   51 
           collimator with a thickness of 0.432 and 0.653 cm,     O0291  1   52 
           respectively. The corresponding areas were 0.183 -     O0291  1   53 
            0.522 cm2 +/- 1.5 %. at some angles, also a 0.1 cm    O0291  1   54 
           thick NE201 scintillator, with an area of 0.353 cm2    O0291  1   55 
            +/- 1.5 %, was used. For the runs at 38.8 MeV the     O0291  1   56 
           same NE102 collimator was used. At 28.8 MeV a 0.13 cm  O0291  1   57 
           thick tantalum collimator, with an area of 0.522 cm    O0291  1   58 
            +/- 1.5 %, was used. The distance from the            O0291  1   59 
           target to the collimator was 45.8 - 47.0 cm +/- 1%.    O0291  1   60 
           The collimator had a misalignment at the center        O0291  1   61 
           of the scattering chamber of +/- 0.5 cm. The precision O0291  1   62 
           of the detector angle was +/- 0.5 degrees. The zero    O0291  1   63 
           angle was determined to +/- 0.5 degrees. The angular   O0291  1   64 
           resolution was +/- 1.2 degrees.                        O0291  1   65 
SAMPLE      Iron target, 3.33 +/- 0.033 mg/cm2 thick, with a      O0291  1   66 
            thickness nonuniformity of +/- 1.5 %. The target      O0291  1   67 
            was enriched to 97.21 % in 54-Fe. The sample was      O0291  1   68 
            oriented with an angular precision of +/- 0.5 degrees.O0291  1   69 
CORRECTION .The Data were corrected for                           O0291  1   70 
            1. Nuclear reactions in the Ge-detector,              O0291  1   71 
            2. Dead layer in the path of the scattered particles, O0291  1   72 
            3. Multiple scattering of particles in the first two  O0291  1   73 
               detectors, which made them miss the total absorp-  O0291  1   74 
               tion detector,                                     O0291  1   75 
            3. Energy loss of the secondary particles in the      O0291  1   76 
               target, and                                        O0291  1   77 
            4. Collimator edge penetration and scattering.        O0291  1   78
